Second Day of the National Vocational Education Conference 88

The Issue of Future Prospects for Young People is the Central Topic

The Result is the Formulation of Two Principles and the Recognition of Three Types of Prospects

丨Morning Group Review丨Afternoon General Assembly Closing丨Today's Tour丨

Resolution Discusses the Organizational Components of the Conference丨Next General Assembly Set for Shenyang or Fujian丨

Vocational Guidance Conference 89

(Zhenjiang Express Report) The National Vocational Discussion Conference, convened by the China Vocational Education Society, was held at Boxian Park in Zhenjiang on the 1st. Details were published in this newspaper. Yesterday (2nd) was the opening date of the National Vocational Guidance Agency Discussion Conference. The address was still Boxian Park. Attended by Chen Xuan’shan, Huang Renzhi, Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, Gao Jian’si, Liu Zhan’en, Liu Yunshou, Zhang Zhongjun, Pan Yinge, Han Yulin, Xu Tai’xian, Zhou Kaisen, Xie Shuping, Xie Jiangcheng, Li Quanshi, Yi Jianlou, Yu Xiaochuan, Liu Jianpan, Pan Yangyao, Yang Chong’gao and other sixty people, led by Chairman Liu Zhan’en to perform the ceremony as usual, and delivered the opening speech, roughly saying that the scope of vocational guidance is very broad, and it is usually a mistake to represent the entire vocational guidance cause with vocational introduction. Vocational guidance is a comprehensive term for vocational research, vocational investigation, vocational introduction, vocational self-cultivation, vocational improvement, etc., and cannot be simply understood as one aspect of vocational introduction. Vocational guidance has only 25 years of history in Europe and the United States. The promotion in China is about 10 years ago. At that time, feeling the importance of this cause and the lack of understanding from the social aspect, a week-long vocational guidance campaign was held in Shanghai, Hankou, Beiping, and Jinan. Later, the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center was established by the China Vocational Education Society, presided over by Mr. Pan Yangyao, and achieved remarkable results. In recent years, places such as Guangdong, Fujian, Liaoning, Hankou, and Tianjin have been planning. Colleagues therefore feel that this cause has recently become more and more developed and that there is a need for unity, so they initiated the Joint Association of Vocational Guidance Agencies. Furthermore, due to the major issues that arise when implementing vocational guidance, first, there is no occupation to guide when implementing vocational guidance; second, what methods are used to implement vocational guidance; third, the timing of vocational guidance, should it be implemented for middle school students or elementary school students; fourth, what kind of people go to implement guidance; and fifth, how to solve economic problems. These five points are recent difficult questions to implement guidance, so they are especially solemnly proposed to contribute to everyone's discussion.

Province Chairman's Representative, He Yushu's Speech (Abridged) 90

I am in charge of agricultural and mining administration and deeply feel the lack of specialized talent. Even with specialized talent, when they handle agricultural and forestry undertakings, they seem to be there to manage administration rather than do the work. They only focus on expanding their personal influence and are unwilling to seek further advancement in their careers. I sincerely hope that those involved in vocational guidance can provide appropriate guidance. The position of vocational guidance organizations in society is like the general staff in the military. Furthermore, I hope that educational institutions, administrative bodies, and society can work together to identify the types of talent needed, so that educational institutions can train such talent to meet practical needs. Following this,

Education Ministry Representative, Gu Shusen's Speech (Abridged): (1) Besides the responsibilities borne by vocational guidance centers, educational institutions must also bear a significant responsibility regarding students' personalities, environments, and various other factors. (2) Those responsible for educational administration should not only focus on building more schools, but also bear significant responsibilities regarding students' career paths after graduation and vocational investigation and analysis. (3) Schools and educational administrative bodies must connect with society to maximize the effectiveness of vocational guidance. Next was the

Reports from Various Vocational Guidance Organizations: Representatives from the Vocational Guidance Federation, the Shanghai Vocational Center, Pan Yangyao, the Nanjing Vocational Guidance Center, Xie Yicheng, the Jiading Vocational Guidance Center, Lu Linxun, the Wuxi Vocational Guidance Center, Rui Ziyu, and the Shanghai YMCA, Zhao Shiying, successively presented reports. After the reports were completed, they began

Discussion of Proposals: Pan Yangyao proposed that a proposal review committee be formed first. The chairman submitted this to a vote, and it was passed. Pan Yangyao, Chen Qingshi, Zhang Zhonghuan, and Li Quanshi were immediately appointed as reviewers. While the proposal review was in progress, the chairman gathered opinions from the entire assembly and raised the issue of young people's career paths for discussion. Chen Qingshi first explained the purpose of discussing this issue, which was not to reach a definitive conclusion but to focus on the improvement of old occupations and the revitalization of new industries in society, as well as the reforms in schools, such as curriculum and facilities, all of which require attention. Li Quanshi then spoke, stating that the issue of young people's career paths is like the marketing of factory products. The success of factory products in the market depends on their durability and practicality. Goods can compete for sales through advertising, and talent can compete for career paths through free competition, which is the examination system. As for expanding career paths, in this era of national rejection of colonialism, going to the frontier, improving old industries, creating new industries, and breaking the favoritism in employment are particularly important. Young people should start their own businesses to solve the career path problem. Gao Jiansi then spoke, stating that recently, some people who have received vocational education cannot find suitable jobs, and those who have jobs cannot maintain them for long, mostly because they lack a service ethic. Therefore, besides vocational education, more emphasis should be placed on character training. Furthermore, primary schools should establish vocational clubs for education, and rural primary schools should serve as the center of rural society, so that graduates of rural primary schools can serve the rural areas. After everyone spoke, the chairman presented a focused argument, summarizing what legitimate career paths young people could have in the future. The atmosphere in the entire assembly became tense. More than twenty people expressed their opinions one after another.

The discussion resulted in a resolution that there were three major career paths for young people in the future: (1) Going back to their hometowns, especially to the countryside. (2) Going to the frontier (such as the Northeast, Northwest, Southwest, and remote areas of their own provinces). (3) Creating new industries and improving old occupations, introducing new occupations. The principles for implementation were: (1) To give young people a sound vocational outlook. (2) To improve school teaching. This proposal was passed after two hours of heated debate. At this time, the proposal review committee had completed its review and submitted the proposals to the general assembly for discussion. The following are excerpts:

Resolutions: (1) This association requests the National Government to issue an order to freeze charitable and relief undertakings in various localities in three phases and convert them into productive employment centers. (2) This association should request the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry to establish national product sales offices nationwide and order all provinces, cities, and counties to simultaneously organize national product collection and sales branches to develop new occupations (proposed by the Changshu Poor Children's Home Product Distribution Office Vocational Guidance Center). It was resolved that the above two proposals be handed over to the executive committee for consideration. (3) This association requests the Central Party Headquarters to order party headquarters in various provinces, cities, and counties to assist in the organization of this association (proposed by the Changshu Poor Children's Home Product Distribution Office Vocational Guidance Center). It was resolved that the association is already in the process of registration and does not need further discussion. (4) This association requests the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to strictly ban speculative activities in exchanges to avoid affecting occupations (proposed by the Changshu Poor Children's Home Product Distribution Office Vocational Guidance Center). It was resolved that it is not within the scope of discussion of this association and should not be included. (5) Encourage schools at all levels to establish more work-study positions (proposed by the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center). It was resolved to pass it and hand it over to the executive committee for handling. (6) Connect with vocational circles to expand career paths for graduates. It was resolved to pass it and hand it over to the executive committee for handling. (7) Advocate for cultivating and colonizing the frontier to open new paths for unemployed youth. It was resolved to pass it and ask the executive committee to discuss specific measures and consider implementing them. (8) Request the Ministry of Education to instruct all provinces and cities to hire as many female faculty members as possible (proposed by the Shanghai Private Aiqun Girls' Middle School).

It was resolved to retain it. It was resolved that the Ministry of Education already has separate regulations, so no separate proposal is needed. (The above six proposals were proposed by Yu Jianqing and Chen Chongyin.) It was resolved that the vocational guidance organizations would be integrated and divided. The rural improvement discussion meeting would be convened and hosted by the Huangxu Rural Improvement Area. The vocational school administration discussion meeting would be convened and hosted by the China Vocational School. The time would be determined by the three organizations. The first proposal was to determine the location of the next meeting. There was a lengthy discussion, and representatives from various regions enthusiastically welcomed the association to hold the general assembly in their region. The final decision was that the first location would be Liaoning, and the second location would be Fujian. After the discussion, the chairmen of each group reported on the group meetings: Liu Jian reported for the vocational education administration group, Jiang Zhuoqun reported for the vocational education curriculum group, Liu Yunchou reported for the agricultural, industrial, and commercial education group, Yang Weiyu reported for the women's vocational education group, and Pan Yangyao et al. successively discussed the proposals. Suspension of Party Membership

Party Rights Not to Stop Public Duties 96

The Ministry of Education instructed the Zhejiang Education Department, stating that regarding the request for instructions on whether party members who are suspended from party rights should also be suspended from their respective public duties, this ministry believes that the matter concerns the punishment of party members and immediately sent a letter to the secretariat of the Central Executive Committee for interpretation. A reply was received, stating roughly that after the revision of the resolution of the Central Standing Committee, it was believed that suspension of party rights could not be equated with expulsion from the party, etc., and the case was recorded and sent to the Executive Yuan for compliance. Therefore, party members who are suspended from party rights should not also be suspended from their respective public duties, etc. In accordance with this, it is ordered that you be informed and instructed to comply.

Japan's First Female Athlete

Kinue Hitomi Passed Away from Illness Yesterday Afternoon 101

丨Suffered from Pleurisy, Treatment for Half a Year Failed

丨Holds a Total of Four World Records

Tokyo, 2nd - Ms. Kinue Hitomi, a famous Japanese female athlete, suffered from pleurisy and was hospitalized at the Osaka Imperial University Hospital. She passed away at 12:25 p.m. on the 2nd at the age of 25.

Sixteen Kinds of Japanese Records 102

Ms. Hitomi was born in the 40th year of Meiji in Fukunari, Fukuura Village, outside Okayama City, Japan. She entered the Japan Women's College of Physical Education and was influenced by Ms. Nikaido, the principal of the school, becoming Japan's only female athlete famous throughout the world. She held Japanese records in sixteen of the seventeen female sports, except for the 80-meter hurdles. She has won countless trophies, gold medals, and silver medals.

Portrait of Kinue Hitomi (Photographed by Ye Changlie) 103

Principal of Her Alma Mater Sheds Tears 104

Ms. Nikaido, the principal of the Japan Women's College of Physical Education, shed tears when she heard the news of Ms. Hitomi's death and told people, "The loss of such a great woman is not only a loss for the world. When will Japan produce a woman like her again? I have no confidence. I am so saddened that I have lost the courage to mention her past."

Ms. Hitomi's Experience 105

Ms. Kinue Hitomi was born on January 1st of the 40th year of Meiji and was the eldest daughter of Mr. Ito Hitomi of Fukunari, Oaza Fukuura Village, Mitsu County, Okayama Prefecture. In March of the 13th year of Taisho, she graduated from the Prefectural Toyama Higher Girls' School. In April of the same year, she entered the Tokyo Nikaido Gymnastics School for Women. In March of the 14th year of Taisho, she graduated. In April of the 15th year of Taisho, she entered the Japan Women's College of Physical Education. In August of the same year, she became the first female athlete in Japan to participate in the Second Women's Summer Games alone (in Gothenburg, Sweden), attracting attention from the sports world around the world. After returning to China, she became an employee of the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun until now. In the 3rd year of Showa, she participated in the Ninth World Olympic Games in Amsterdam, Netherlands. Last May, she went to Prague, Czechoslovakia, to participate in the Third Women's Olympic Games. At the end of the 5th year of Showa, she fell ill. In May of this year, her condition became serious, and she passed away today.

A Word of Wisdom 108

— Chonglou

Credit and reputation are equally important to a person. If you cherish your reputation, you must first maintain your credit. If you are down on your luck, never expect someone to come to your rescue. But if you are successful, you should try to help others.

A loyal friend is like a cotton-padded coat. It seems annoying and useless in the hot summer, but it becomes indispensable in the cold winter.

Most fallen men are created by bad women. Most fallen women are created by bad men.

Life is about satisfying desires. But in this era of the class system, the desires of life will never be satisfied.

Those who like to take advantage always end up suffering.

Planting causes is like planting fruits. Planting peach pits yields sweet fruits, planting plum pits yields bitter fruits.

Repairing Yan Ziling's Fishing Platform 109

— Zizai

Yan Ziling of Yuyao in the Eastern Han Dynasty studied with Guangwu in his youth. When Guangwu ascended the throne, he changed his name and hid himself. The emperor ordered someone to search for him and found him. He was offered the position of Counselor, but he declined. He farmed on Mount Fuchun. Later generations named his fishing spot Yanling Shoal, also known as Qili Rapids, in Tonglu, Zhejiang. It stretches for seven li, with mountains on both sides and the water rushing like an arrow. There is a saying that "with wind, seven li; without wind, seventy li," meaning that it is difficult to tow boats, and the speed depends on the wind. However, the scenery is excellent. Unfortunately, due to the passage of time, various constructions have fallen into disrepair. Historical sites and scenic spots are covered in weeds, which diminishes the interest of visitors. Recently, Wang Kun, Yu Shaosong, Zhao Jinqing, Lu Bofan, Lu Zhushuang, Qu Yingguang, and others initiated a restoration project. The estimated cost is 30,000 gold yuan. Each initiator contributed 500 yuan, and the rest was solicited from all walks of life. Wang Zhengting, Shao Lizi, Wang Xiaolai, and others have supported the project, which is now actively underway and scheduled to begin construction by the end of the year. In the future, the fishing platform will be renewed, and Mr. Yan's character will be as towering as the mountains and as long as the rivers. The text of the reconstruction announcement is elegant and grand, and is recorded below to inform those who understand.

I have heard that Yingyang Gao Dao did not yield to Fangxun's humble request to return the government, and that Guzhu Qingbiao ultimately declined Qizhou's offer of a thatched cottage. Therefore, chiseling blanks to attract the departed, the Marquis of Wei was still seen rejected by Duangan, and listening to falsehoods to resign, the Lord of Lu could not obtain Yan He. The meaning of hermitage is not far from ancient times. In this corrupt world, the custom has gradually declined. Yanling of Fuchun is where Mr. Yan of Han Dynasty used to fish. Beside it is the Yuxitai of Xie Gao of the Song Dynasty. Mr. Yan upheld the principle of not serving the court and cherished the ambition of longevity. He lived in the fields and was haggard on the rivers and seas. His legacy is known among the common people. The construction of temples for sacrifices has long been a practice. The comrades and others took advantage of their spare time and pondered on distant thoughts. They rowed up the Tongjiang River and looked up at this temple. They cherished the feelings of a bygone era in the old ruins and were moved by the solitude of a lonely world in the desolate pavilion. It is a pity that the world has been far away for generations, and the spiritual abode has been declining. The Star Pavilion is desolate, and the Xifa Pavilion is deserted. It has not been repaired since the 55th year of Kangxi of the Qing Dynasty. The members and others have not only appreciated the beauty of the scenery but have also admired it deeply. Therefore, they made a wish to repair it and use grand structures. The materials must be firm, and the regulations must be simple. They also thought of planting more pines and cypresses to enhance the view, and to widen the steps for climbing. However, this great undertaking will cost a lot. Therefore, a short letter is written to jointly support this grand event. The clouds, mountains, rivers, and waters dare to compare with Fan Gong's achievements. The red lychees and yellow bananas are attached to Han Yu's righteousness.

Competition of Go Masters 110

— Xiaocao

The winner of the first place can win a prize of 800 yuan

The Chinese Go Club on Sapo Road in this city has been established for three months. There are many enthusiastic members. In order to increase the interest of the members, the club has launched a large-scale competition to examine the achievements of each player and to seek deeper artistic cultivation. Mr. Zhang Danru and Mr. Sheng Zecheng, the vice presidents of the club, took the lead in donating cash to reward the winners. At that time, the competition will be divided into two groups, A and B. (That is, Group A will compete with Group A, and Group B will compete with Group B. Groups A and B will not compete with each other.) The organization of each group's level will be based on the club's general secretary, Mr. Liu Dihuai, as the standard, and he will judge whether they are Group A or B. Those who play Even with Mr. Liu or Mr. Liu gives first are assigned to Group A. If Mr. Liu gives two stones, they are assigned to Group B. Each group will consist of 10 people, and each person will play 27 games. The competition will last for one month. Each group will select three winners. The champion of Group A will receive a prize of 800 yuan, the second place will receive 400 yuan, and the third place will receive 200 yuan. The first place in Group B will receive 300 yuan, the second place will receive 200 yuan, and the third place will receive 100 yuan. Several rules for the game will be formulated, and the club's president, Mr. Du Shenchen, will be publicly elected as the chief judge. Currently, it is feared that players from other cities may not be able to arrive in time. (There are many masters in the Pingjin area.) Therefore, the competition is tentatively scheduled to begin in mid-August and end in mid-September. Those who are hidden in the mountains and forests and possess superb Go skills can register with the club and join the competition. At that time, masters from all over the country will gather together to compete for the championship. This unprecedented event will be very spectacular.

Yarn and Cotton: In addition to a drop of three taels in the spot price of yarn last week, current sales are booming... with 15,000 bales sold. The yarn market was relatively stable at the beginning of the week, and the development of coarse yarn trading between the Guangdong and Yunnan gangs led to a slight strengthening of sentiment. However, the overseas cotton market was trending downwards, so sentiment was dull. In addition, Japanese yarn suddenly became active, and trading started again, revealing a weakening trend in the market. Later, with the Factory Law taking effect on August 1st, the market situation slightly improved. However, the third-grade yarn and the American and Indian cotton markets continued to decline, showing a significant downward trend. At the same time, the tense situation in the northern war zone and the sharp drop in raw cotton caused the yarn market to fundamentally loosen, and the downward trend was sharp. The market was thus in a slump. As for the actual demand side, seeing the unfavorable environment, they were all hesitant to move forward, and business was greatly affected. In addition, due to floods in various areas, autumn sales were affected, so there were many sellers. However, due to weak base stocks and the pessimism of the world cotton industry, it was difficult to recover due to the pressure. The total transaction volume of labeled yarn throughout the week was 194,100 bales, and the prices for each month fell by more than three taels compared to the previous week. Among the customer gangs, current sales were still good, with each gang buying a total of 13,210 bales. Among the peers, 1,600 bales were entered. The selling price fell by 1.2 taels. Last week, the Han cotton price rose sharply and then fell, resulting in a drop of 1.89 qian compared to the previous weekend. At the beginning of last week, the cotton market was affected by floods in various areas, with more cotton fields being submerged. Moreover, the continuous rain made people worry about the prospects of new cotton, so everyone was bullish, and inland gangs came to Shanghai to purchase futures in large quantities, causing the market to be extremely excited. As a result, there was a period of rising prices. Before long, the weather cleared up, and the floodwaters receded slightly. However, the losses were already significant. The world cotton market was also unfavorable, with a sharp downward trend and pressure far exceeding that of the floods. Moreover, the gold price was fluctuating, and the calculation of the silver price of foreign cotton was low. As a result, the cotton market was greatly affected, and the local and foreign machine gangs sold off together. Once there was bad news, the reaction was even sharper. The highest price of labeled cotton in August was 39 taels, and the lowest price last week was 36.15 taels, which shows the magnitude of the change. At the end of the week, labeled cotton was showing new low prices step by step due to the frequent decline of American cotton. Indian cotton had a tendency to come to Guangdong, and Shenxin had already purchased 4,000 pieces, causing buyers to be uneasy, and retail investors were in a state of terror. Japanese merchants were also selling, and the market was falling wildly and uncontrollably. The prices for each month fell by 1.89 qian compared to the previous week, and the transaction volume was 587,800 dan. They resolved to organize a petition delegation. The Bureau of Commodity Inspection of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is implementing inspection of exported tea leaves. Previously, the foreign firms had stated their reasons and expressed their opposition, and notified the tea warehouses, stating that in addition to returning the original barrel of tea that failed to pass the inspection, they would also be responsible for various unlimited losses. Chinese tea merchants are in this season of tea industry decline, and have no extra strength to resist the foreign firms. They are deeply worried that the export of colored tea will be prohibited in the future, and the local shops will not be able to sell it. All the capital of the merchants will inevitably be lost. Therefore, a second plenary meeting was convened at the Foreign Firms Tea Industry Association a few days ago, and it was resolved to organize a petition delegation and submit a document to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and the Bureau of Commodity Inspection, requesting the cancellation of the inspection of exported tea leaves. Local News: The High Court and the Special Second District Court to Open Today - Trial of Cases Referred by the Police - Announcement of Personnel for Both Courts - According to the Daily News, the Third Branch of the High Court and the Second Special District Local Court have been established since August 1st. Internal matters, including the receipt of documents and miscellaneous items from the French Public Concession, have been generally checked. The two courts are scheduled to start working today. If there are cases referred by the police, trials will be held immediately. The news obtained yesterday is recorded below: - Yesterday's Situation: Yesterday, the funds, files, and other items received by the two courts from the French side were completely handed over and checked. They are currently undergoing sorting. As for the prison, the French guards inside have been withdrawn. In order to understand the past history, a small number of French guards have been left at the entrance for inquiries at any time. - Official Opening: The two courts will open today, and the working hours are set from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 1:00 PM to 4:00 PM. Due to the initial establishment, everything needs to be sorted out, so there is no summer vacation like other courts. Starting today, all staff members who come to the courts must sign in. - Trial of Cases Today: Cases are scheduled to be tried from the 6th, but important civil and criminal cases may be tried at any time. If there are cases referred by the French police today, they will be investigated immediately. - Appointment of Du Ge: Du Ge, the former French assessor of the French Public Concession, has expressed his willingness to serve as a consultant after the establishment of our courts. Mr. Du has expressed this intention to President Liang of the High Court Branch. Yesterday, President Liang obtained an appointment from the Ministry of Judicial Administration and officially appointed Mr. Du as a consultant to the court. From now on, Mr. Du will contribute his years of experience in the French Public Concession as a reference for the operation of the High Court and the Special Court. - Announcement of Personnel: The list of personnel for the two courts was partially announced previously, and it was not complete. Yesterday, the reporter of the Daily News inquired from President Liang about the full list of personnel. The Third Branch of the High Court includes President Liang Renjie, Chief Prosecutor Peng Wangye, Criminal Division Chief Liang Jian, Civil Division Chief Wang Gangxu, Judges Zhao Zhenhai, Xu Wenrong, Guo Dezhang, Candidate Judges Li Changnian, Zhang Chaozuo, Prosecutor Zhang Keru, Chief Clerk Tang Zaili, Director of the Prosecutor's Office, Clerk Liu Nean, Clerks Tan Shou Gong, Liu Jiayi, Yin Tingji, Luo Zongyang, Peng Jianbiao, Shi Ji, He Shaolin, Qiu Hu, Candidate Clerks Zeng Fanzhen, Ren Qirong, Zou Wenxuan, Wu Hengben, Zhou Shuren, and Student Clerks Song Xianru, Wang Rongxi, Li Shu. As for the personnel of the Special Court, it has not been officially announced yet. Yesterday, the reporter of the Daily News inquired from various parties about the full list of staff, including President Ying Shi, Civil Division Chief Ying Jian, Criminal Division Chief Ge Zhitan, Judges Xiong Huiping, Pang Shurong, Luo Renji, Qu Cengze, Candidate Judges Zhang Jinjian, Zhang Jiongguang, Wu Fanglian, Ma Shounan, Shao Mengtong, Zhu Ganlin, Zhang Chaozuo (also of the Third Branch of the High Court), Li Changnian (also of the Third Branch of the High Court), Prosecutor Lou Guanguang, Candidate Prosecutors Ding Jìmèng, Xie Zhijing, Chief Clerk Xiao Jinfang, and Clerks Su Jingqi, Huang Mingmin, Han Jinxiang, Feng Meixue, Feng Bangyan, Wei Yuwei, and Li Zhuhua. The Wonderful Method of Sanctioning the Happiness Chain 112

— Jing Bo

Recently, there has been a kind of "happiness chain" spreading throughout the country. As far as I am concerned, I have received no less than several dozen such chains from friends within a week. This kind of chain was also received several times in the past few years, but most of them were in English or French, with Chinese ones being extremely rare. Unexpectedly, this year, the gentlemen and ladies of the whole country actually regard it as a fashionable undertaking, sending them out in large quantities. The reason for this is unknown. Social figures are currently studying methods of sanctioning it. Mr. Zhu Hongda, a famous lawyer in Shanghai, recently published a letter he sent to a friend in response to receiving a chain, the wording of which is extraordinarily humorous and quite reasonable. If various circles can follow suit, this kind of meaningless superstition can naturally be eliminated invisibly. The original letter is recorded below. (Omitted above) We haven't communicated for a long time. Suddenly, I received your grand communication. Reading its content, I know that you sent the letter to me because of superstition. This time, social figures are engaging in mutually forwarding happiness chains, which can be said to be extremely meaningless. If each of those who sent them is ignored by colleagues, it is fine, but in your case, you actually printed nine copies for distribution, so I must warn you. I ask, can the lives and deaths of colleagues be affected by curses? You must know that scholars don't have time to research the problem of life and death. The progress of modern medical physiology is advancing by leaps and bounds. As for collapsing houses, it is even more absurd. Whether a house is solid or not is based on the principles of engineering. You are actually so superstitious. You should know that superstition violates science. This kind of behavior not only wastes your own resources, but also needlessly increases the labor of the post office, affecting society. My method of warning you is to forward the two copies you sent back to you. If you believe in it, you must print eighteen copies for distribution. It would be best if, among the eighteen copies, you send back two copies to me again, so that I can return them to you as before. You would probably have no peaceful days. If you agree with my idea, then quickly destroy the remaining seven copies. (Omitted below)

The Tragic Situation of the Great Flood in Wuzhen 113

— Rui Hongchu

Recently, it has been raining continuously for half a month. A few days ago, I returned to my hometown of Wuzhen on business. Day after day, the wind and rain raged, the river water rose sharply, the fields were submerged, and boats were cut off from traffic due to the high water level under the bridges. With nothing to do in the rainy window, I hereby record the tragic situation of the great flood that I witnessed, as follows.

The Streets are a Vast Expanse of Water The heavy rain has lasted for half a month, and the river water has risen sharply. In low-lying areas, it has spread to the streets, starting from the Labor Family Wharf in Dongzha and ending at Xiaowuzhen. In places like the Ji Family Estuary in Nanzha, the accumulated water is several feet deep. Moreover, there are no fewer than several thousand buildings along the river that are all submerged in the water, resembling a vast expanse of water. It is pitiful.

It is Difficult to Walk on the Floating Bridges In the town, such as the Yan Ting Nei Nong, Caishen Bay, and Sanli Tang, the streets are covered with several inches of accumulated water. The wide roads are filled with the sighs of "I can't walk, brother!" So, wooden floating bridges are built to facilitate transportation. Modern girls, wearing high-heeled leather shoes, exclaim "It's hard to walk!" non-stop when crossing the floating bridges.

Men and Women Scoop Water Day and Night The majority of farmers in the countryside rely on farming for a living. This time, they suddenly suffered a natural disaster, and the fields are about to be submerged. Therefore, farmers, both men and women, scoop water day and night without stopping, enduring hardship. It is extremely unfortunate.

Reports of Floods from Various Villages Since the torrential rain on July 6th, it has been more than twenty days, and it has been continuously raining. The water level rises daily. Hundreds of acres of rice fields in the surrounding villages have all become a swamp. If the weather clears and the water recedes, it may still be possible to salvage the situation. Unexpectedly, it has continued to rain in recent days, and the water is rising severely in secret. The phenomenon of flooding has already formed. There will be no harvest of rice in the farmland. Therefore, farmers are flocking to the county government to report the flood, one after another.

Rice Prices Soar Daily The river water is high, and the source of rice and grain is scarce. Rice merchants are taking the opportunity to raise rice prices, increasing the price per dan by one yuan, with two increases in one day. Therefore, the rice merchants are all smiles, while the common people suffer.

News from the Art World Mr. Yu Tongfu, Mr. Guan Yide, Mr. Chen Juanyin, and Mr. Xu Kangmin are the four outstanding figures in the painting world of Wuzhong. Their landscapes enter Song and Yuan dynasties through the Four Wangs, and their flower-and-bird paintings acquire the lost meaning of Chong Si. Their brushwork is exquisite and their ink is wonderful. People in Wu are so addicted to them that it has become a habit. However, due to their duties, the four gentlemen, although like-minded, often experience separation. One day two weeks ago, the four suddenly met at the co-drinking ice room in the park. They expressed their feelings of separation and chatted happily. Due to the difficulty of gathering together, they decided to collaborate on a hundred pages of fan leaves to commemorate this encounter. The news spread, and the quota was full in less than three days. Upon request, they increased the quota by fifty. But in less than a day, it was full again. After repeated requests from various parties, they reluctantly agreed to collaborate on a hundred hanging scrolls to forge ink bonds.

Travel Notes of India (73) 114

— Linghua

The fourth was the day of the Indian New Year festival. At nine o'clock, the students officially performed the painting and splashing water rituals. They went to the head of the school one by one, and the head of the school performed the ritual for each of them. There were two kinds of rituals. One, each student took red powder and painted the head of the school's forehead. Second, the head of the school performed the ritual of connecting left and right shoulders with each student. Think about it, each student painted once, and there were hundreds of students. Then the head of the school's head and face can be imagined. The Indian university system is that a university has a president, and there are six or seven departments under him. Each department has a head of the school who has full authority to handle everything. There is no title of president. The students sprinkle colored water on each other. Some came to paint my face. I only allowed them to dot my forehead. But if everyone came, it would be a great suffering. So I closed the door and didn't go out. After a while, someone knocked on the door to perform the painting ritual, with great sincerity. They asked me if China had this custom. I replied, "No." I heard that France has a flower-scattering party. Every festival, all the citizens go out to play and throw flowers at each other. The flowers fall on the ground, several inches thick. India has many flowers. If the ritual of sprinkling water and painting faces is changed to scattering flowers, it would be more fragrant, elegant, and interesting. The students said, "We know that this custom is not very good. Our bodies are covered with dirt. Our clothes cannot be worn. The whole country is crazy. But it is not easy to change." This is an Indian custom. I said, "In today's world, everything is being renewed. You can write articles and publish them in newspapers to advocate it. You must renew customs to seek evolution." The reason for painting faces is rooted in religion. All Indians who paint their faces are practitioners, representing closeness to God. Now, imitating and promoting it, everyone paints it during the New Year to express closeness to God, which is a very auspicious ritual. It is rooted in faith, so it is not easy to reform. But it seems not difficult to replace it with scattering flowers. After performing the painting ritual, they still have to be given candy, like paying New Year's greetings in our country. So young people are more happy to do this movement.

We indirectly read Indian history from English, and it is difficult to remember its people's names and place names. Indian people's names are especially difficult to remember. It is very different from the simplicity of Chinese names. What I object to most is Indian writing. Although I know that a friend said how good Sanskrit is, but watching the repeated redundancy of the Buddhist scriptures, I dislike it very much, and what I hate most is its people's names. Often with acquaintances of many days, I cannot call their names. This is not the stupidity of the Chinese, but the stupidity of the Indian language. However, Indian people's names all have deep philosophical and religious meanings. We love its meaning but hate its name.

According to Indian history, Buddhism flourished in the sixth century BC and declined in the twelfth century AD. Hinduism revived. Therefore, the prevalence of Buddhism in India lasted for 1,800 years. It has been gone for more than 700 years now. In the future, there will be a tendency to revive. In 273 BC, King Ashoka unified the five Indias and sent his younger siblings to Ceylon to preach. I asked a friend from Ceylon to tell the truth, and he did not believe that the Buddha had personally been to Ceylon. However, there are records of preaching on Mount Lanka. Perhaps the Buddha went by boat, which is not difficult. I dare not easily believe in myths of flight and incarnation. King Ashoka was the only saintly king. History says that he built official roads, planted mango trees, built public wells, and promoted loyalty and filial piety. There were no criminals in the whole country. It was the rule of Yao and Shun. However, a monk told me that King Ashoka did not believe in Buddhism at first. When he was using troops, he wanted to kill a bhikkhu. The bhikkhu was not afraid at all. The king asked him why he was not afraid of death. He replied that it was because he understood life and death. The king then asked about the Buddha's teachings and was moved to believe in Buddhism.

Speaking Club, Rotary Club

Women Women (8) 115

— Yao Sufeng

Before he could answer, his mother couldn't help but interject. She had originally thought that since Xiao Rong had returned, he would stay for a day or two before leaving, but now hearing him say that he was leaving immediately, she was naturally very unhappy. So she also pleaded with Xiao Rong to stay. However, Xiao Rong always expressed that he had to leave.

His father, too, felt that it was inappropriate for Xiao Rong to return to Shanghai immediately. He firmly said, "No! You come back only to ask for money, and once you get the money, you want to leave. Putting aside that you are my son and I am your father, if I ask you to go tomorrow, you must obey. Even if you were my elder, and I were your junior, if I begged you to go tomorrow, shouldn't you at least give me some face?" He was clearly a bit angry. Xiao Rong was speechless.

However, Xiao Rong still felt that he had to leave. No matter his wife's entreaties, his mother's persuasion, or his father's orders, all failed. His father finally became furious. "Fine! Let him go! You don't need to talk to him anymore." After saying that, he walked outside.

Xiao Rong's wife was almost about to cry, but Xiao Rong, without turning his head, followed his father stiffly and walked out, without saying a single word of farewell, nor even looking at them.

Xiao Rong finally left in his father's carriage. His mother and wife saw him off at the door, but he didn't seem to notice them. When the carriage had driven far away, shrinking from the entire carriage and people to a tiny black dot, they still stretched their necks and gazed into the distance. After a while, everything disappeared from their sight. The mother-in-law and daughter-in-law could only sigh in unison and lazily walked inside.

On the other side, the carriage had already arrived at the station. Xiao Rong got out of the carriage and finally said a few words to his father: "Dad! I'm leaving! I'll come back as soon as I have time!"

"You must study hard in school. When you read a book, you must think about where the money for your studies comes from. Go and do well! Don't be lazy and love to play, and disappoint our good intentions!"

Xiao Rong nodded and walked into the crowd. Although his father felt very angry, when he thought that he had been pulling a carriage hard for fifteen years and had made no progress, and that he only had such a son, and all his hopes were on him, he smiled slightly to himself.

The train departed. Xiao Rong, who had arrived in a third-class carriage, was now sitting proudly in a second-class carriage, drinking soda and eating Western food. Who would know where his money came from?

Three hours later, the magnificent Shanghai shone in Xiao Rong's eyes again, and he regained his vibrancy from the day before. Everything about his home had disappeared in the turning of the wheels. He didn't want to think about it anymore, and he wouldn't think about it anymore.

Complicated Gold Market Last Week 117

Fell by Seven Taels and Seven Mace Compared to the Previous Weekend

Reversal from Sharp Rise to Setback, Fluctuating by Twenty-Two Taels The gold market last week saw violent fluctuations, turning from a sharp rise to a setback, with frequent ups and downs. At the beginning of the week, it once surged above 750 taels, reaching 58.5 taels, due to the sharp fall in the silver market. However, due to the poor environment, with news that Mexico was changing to silver coins and stopping gold coins, people seemed to be bearish, causing the bulls to dare not do it in advance, so it was difficult to break through the 60-tael mark. Afterwards, the trend went downstream, forming a situation of hovering. By Thursday, large households sold off aggressively, causing a sudden drop to 736.5 taels. Afterwards, it hovered around 40 taels, with a total difference of 22 taels. Overall, it fell back by 7.7 taels. As for domestic and foreign silver markets and drafts, the statistics only showed a slight increase, but there was no important news. The buying and selling by both bulls and bears in the industry seemed to be quite different. According to the closing price on the exchange rate, it was around 50 taels. The spot red bar sales market was still active, with Tianjin and other gangs buying every day, so the price ranged from 9.5 taels to over 11 taels (calculated by progressively adding the gold price). However, the inventory was full, with about 30,000 bars, which may have suppressed the gold price. The public bill (August futures) began to be collected on Saturday (August 1st), with about 8,000 bars collected on the first day. The collectors were mostly spot dealers. Therefore, the rise and fall of the future gold price is difficult to predict, and there may still be a change. It is said that Germany will issue silver coins, but the raw silver needed is from previous inventory, so the price of silver will not rise in the short term. The general situation of this week is summarized below.

Mexico's Change to Silver Coins Gradually Trending Downward Since Monday (July 27), the large silver bar retreated 3.125, the American silver retreated 3.75, the advance order retreated half a stop, and the domestic market was also tight. The industry rushed to make settlements. The opening of the September gold price immediately rose to 756 taels. American stocks fell, and there were many buyers, so it was 58.5 taels. Later, due to the sale by Wu and others, it plunged by more than 5 taels. Luo competed to buy it, so it rose by 4 or 5 taels. In the afternoon, the advance order appeared loose, and the bank was quite willing to sell it, and finally broke through 50 taels, calculated as 49.5 taels, closing at 52.7 mace, which had risen for three consecutive days, totaling 3.2 mace. However, due to the saying that Mexico changed to silver coins, it was difficult to break through 60 taels, and it repeatedly went downstream. The next day, the large silver bar rebounded by half a penny, and the silver price also increased by half a cent. The advance order only increased by half a stop, the domestic market also loosened, and Chinese merchants still dumped. The situation was the opposite of the previous day. The gold market opened at 742 taels, plunging by 10.07 mace. Then, due to the stable foundation of the large bar, and America was willing to sell at the listed price of 0.0625, it rebounded by more than 4 mace. After that, it was flat, with slight advances and retreats. In the afternoon, it was even flatter, closing at 45 taels, retreating by 7.7 mace. On Wednesday, the large bar retreated by 0.25, and the silver price of 1.25 advance order did not change. The price was stable in both the open and the hidden markets. The gold market opened at 44.5 mace and rebounded by a small 5 mace, due to someone maintaining the foundation. Then it retreated to 43 taels. Due to the diligent buying, it rose to 47 taels. In the afternoon, it reached 3.5 taels, closing at 4.8 mace, only decreasing by 2 mace. Because the draft market was closed on Wednesday, the gold market was also flat. The next day, the large bar did not change, and the gold market opened at 46.5, slightly increasing by 1.7 mace. Later, large households such as Ying and Luo sold off, suddenly breaking through 40 taels, only counting 37 taels. Then it increased by 3 or 4 taels. In the afternoon, it was finally flat at 36 taels, due to the report of an increase in the Indian exchange rate. Then it was 40 taels, closing still calculated at 38.5 taels, which had been decreasing for three consecutive days, totaling 6.3 mace, with a total of 10.2 mace in fluctuation throughout the day. On Friday, the large bar saw an increase of 0.125, the silver price increased by 0.25, the advance order did not change, and the domestic market did not change. Many in the industry made settlements. The gold price opened with a rebound of 1.5 mace, calculated at 40 taels, which was said to be due to the Bank of England raising interest rates to avoid the outflow of cash, so people were bullish. Later, due to the sale by the Dalian gang, it seemed to decline, to 37.2 taels. After that, it hovered around 40 taels. In the afternoon, it reached 43.7 mace, because the advance order became firmer, only settling at 0.125 to 0.0625, closing at 43.4 mace, rebounding by 4.9 mace compared to the previous day. On Saturday, the large bar fell by 0.0625, the silver market fell by 0.125, the advance order did not change, and the domestic market seemed to loosen. The gold market opened slightly smaller by 4 mace, at 43 taels, because the silver market had shrunk a lot. Then, from 2.2 mace, it increased to 3.7 mace. Afterwards, the trend weakened, and the supply was greater than the demand, finally being 38 taels. At noon, due to the small report of the Indian exchange rate, it increased to 43.2 mace. When closing, it was 41.8 mace, retreating by 1.6 mace compared to the previous day. However, after closing, it was suppressed again by about 2 mace, to around 40 taels to 41 taels, with a fluctuation of 5.7 mace in half a day. The British, American, and Indian silver markets and exchange rates are described separately below.
